## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of current population P and time t, which is the central problem in mathematical population ecology. The growth rate typically depends on P through density-dependent feedback mechanisms, and on t through environmental forcing or seasonal effects.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent unlimited growth)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth decelerating logarithmically near carrying capacity)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with flexible inflection point)
- Strong Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth negative below critical threshold c1)
- Weak Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 + P) (reduced per-capita growth at low density without extinction threshold)
- Beverton-Holt continuous form: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (saturating density dependence)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism-catabolism balance growth model)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (generalized sigmoid growth)
- Seasonal logistic: dP_dt = c0 * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * P * (1 - c3 * P) (logistic with periodic environmental forcing)
- Harvesting model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (logistic growth with constant harvesting)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (fractional power density dependence)
- Exponential decay with immigration: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 (linear growth/decline with constant immigration)
- Cubic density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (polynomial density-dependent feedback)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Multiplicative P factor → Conservation of 'no growth without population': dP/dt must vanish when P=0, so P typically appears as a multiplicative factor
- Quadratic P terms (P - P²) → Density-dependent self-limitation producing logistic-type saturation at carrying capacity
- Cubic P terms (P² - P³ or P·(P-a)·(1-P/K)) → Allee effects where very small populations have negative growth rates
- Logarithmic coupling log(K/P) → Gompertz-type asymmetric growth where deceleration near carrying capacity differs from acceleration at low density
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) modulating growth rate → Seasonal or periodic environmental forcing on reproduction/mortality
- Ratio P/(1+c*P) → Saturating per-capita resource competition where individual growth rate plateaus rather than linearly declining
- Fractional power P**c with 0<c<1 → Surface-area-to-volume scaling effects in organismal or colonial growth
- Additive constant term independent of P → Immigration, stocking, or constant harvesting external to population dynamics
- Product of multiple linear factors in P → Multiple equilibria / multi-stability in population dynamics (extinction, intermediate, carrying capacity)
- Time-dependent exponential envelope exp(c*t) multiplying growth terms → Gradually changing environmental conditions or resource depletion over time
